#### Opcodes

```
  0: 0x0628 [0x33] EventEntity->Render.Flags0 |= 0x200000 // Bit 21 (flag=0x01)
  1: 0x062A [0x37] UPDATE_EVENT_POSITION_AND_DIR: x=-6.123*, z=-69.317*, y=-4.000*, direction=87.9°*
  2: 0x0633 [0x00] END_REQSTACK()
```
